style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"http://advocate.asla.org/app/sign-petition?0&amp;engagementId=334973\"><h2>Stand Up for Science-based Policy Making</h2></a><p>This year, Earth Day coincides with the March for Science. Sign ASLA's letter, which we will deliver to EPA administrator Scott Pruitt.</p><p class=\"bylineText\">Earth from space / istockphoto.com</p></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 313px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/studentawards.jpg&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/studentawards.jpg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"/2017cfe/index.html\"><h2>Student Awards Call for Entries</h2></a><p>Submissions are due May 15.</p><p class=\"bylineText\">ASLA 2016 Student General Design Honor Award. The Digital &amp; the Wild: Mitigating Risk Through Landscape Adaptation / Jordan Duke, University of Toronto</p></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 313px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/WLAM-TILA995.jpg?n=9115&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/WLAM-TILA995.jpg?n=9115\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"https://www.asla.org/ContentDetail.aspx?id=45783\"><h2>World Landscape Architecture Month (WLAM)</h2></a><p>Join the Celebration!</p><p class=\"bylineText\">ASLA 2015 Professional General Design Award of Excellence. At the Hudson's Edge: Beacon's Long Dock a Resilient Riverfront Park, Reed Hilderbrand LLC / James Ewing Photography</p></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 313px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/uptown%20normal.jpg&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/uptown%20normal.jpg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"https://www.asla.org/NewsReleaseDetails.aspx?id=50078\"><h2>Our Statement on President Trump's Budget</h2></a><p>We are disappointed with President Trumps budget blueprint, which calls for dramatic cuts. Read the full statement.</p><p class=\"bylineText\">Transit-oriented, multi-modal development in Uptown Normal Illinois, financed by 2010 TIGER grant / U.S. Department of Transportation</p></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 313px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/2017InfrastructureProposal.jpg?n=5634&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/2017InfrastructureProposal.jpg?n=5634\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"/NewsReleaseDetails.aspx?id=50061\"><h2>Our Infrastructure Priorities </h2></a><p>ASLA urges policy makers and stakeholders to support an infrastructure plan that not only addresses todays crumbling infrastructure, but also creates tomorrows resilient systems.</p><p class=\"bylineText\">Queens Plaza in Queens NYC, 2012 / Sam Oberter</p></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 313px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/ASLACLA.jpg&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/ASLACLA.jpg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"/center.aspx\"><h2>ASLA Center for Landscape Architecture</h2></a><p>ASLA has moved into the new ASLA Center for Landscape Architecture. Learn how the design improves sustainability and employee health and wellness.</p><p class=\"bylineText\">ASLA Center for Landscape Architecture conceptual drawing / Gensler</p></div></li></ul>\n          \n            <a href=\"\" class=\"uk-slidenav showArrow\" data-uk-slideshow-item=\"previous\"><img src=\"/images/slideshow-prev.png\"></a>\n            <a href=\"\" class=\"uk-slidenav showArrow uk-slidenav-next\" data-uk-slideshow-item=\"next\"><img src=\"/images/slideshow-next.png\"></a>\n            <ul class=\"uk-dotnav uk-dotnav-contrast uk-position-bottom\"><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"0\" class=\"uk-active\"><a href=\"\"></a></li><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"1\"><a href=\"\"></a></li><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"2\"><a href=\"\"></a></li><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"3\"><a href=\"\"></a></li><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"4\"><a href=\"\"></a></li><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"5\"><a href=\"\"></a></li></ul>\n            \n        </div>\n    </div>\n<div id=\"learn-what-la-do\" class=\"uk-modal\">\n    <div class=\"uk-modal-dialog uk-modal-dialog-blank\">\n        <a class=\"uk-modal-close uk-close\"></a>\n        <div class=\"uk-slidenav-position\" data-uk-slideshow=\"{autoplay:true}\">\n            <div class=\"uk-modal-header\">\n\n                <div class=\"modal--title\">\n                    <img src=\"/images/asla-light-logo.png\">\n                    <h1>This is Landscape Architecture:</h1>\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"learnAnchors\"><div><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"0\" class=\"uk-active\"><a>Parks</a></li><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"1\"><a>Campuses</a></li><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"2\"><a>Memorials</a></li><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"3\"><a>Reuse</a></li><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"4\"><a>Residential Design</a></li></div><div><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"5\"><a>Urban Revitalization</a></li><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"6\"><a>Rain Gardens</a></li><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"7\"><a>Ecological Restoration</a></li><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"8\"><a>Green Roofs</a></li><li data-uk-slideshow-item=\"9\"><a>Transportation</a></li></div></div>\n\n            </div>\n            <ul class=\"uk-slideshow uk-overlay-active\" style=\"height: 0px;\"><li aria-hidden=\"false\" class=\"uk-active\" style=\"height: 0px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Hunters-Point-South.jpg&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Hunters-Point-South.jpg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"https://www.asla.org/2014awards/467.html\"><h2>Parks</h2></a><p>In Queens, New York, the next generation of waterfront park is here. Hunter's Point South by Thomas Balsley Associates and Weiss Manfredi shows how cities can transform their industrial waterfronts into healthy community magnets that will outlast any storm.</p><label class=\"bylineText\">ASLA 2014 General Design Honor Award. Hunter's Point South. Thomas Balsley Associates and Weiss Manfredi / image credit: Wade Zimmerman</label></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 0px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Salem-State-University.jpg&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Salem-State-University.jpg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"https://www.asla.org/2014awards/164.html\"><h2>Campuses</h2></a><p>At Salem State University in Massachusetts, a new residence hall offered the perfect opportunity for WagnerHodgson Landscape Architect to improve the campus' ecological health. A courtyard and green roof absorb stormwater runoff, protecting the nearby marsh from pollution.</p><label class=\"bylineText\">ASLA 2014 Professional General Design Honor Award. Salem State University  Marsh Hall, Salem, Massachusetts. WagnerHodgson Landscape Architecture / image credit: Robert Benson</label></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 0px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Gebran-Tueni-Memorial.jpg&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Gebran-Tueni-Memorial.jpg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"https://www.asla.org/2014awards/059.html\"><h2>Memorials</h2></a><p>In Beirut, Lebanon, the scene of decades of violence, a new memorial by Vladimir Djurovic Landscape Architecture honors Gebran Tueni, a journalist assassinated by a car bomb. Stones etched with his name are meant to be taken, as they are continuously replenished.</p><label class=\"bylineText\">ASLA 2014 Professional General Design Honor Award. Gebran Tueni Memorial. Beirut Central District, Beirut, Lebanon. Vladimir Djurovic Landscape Architecture / Image credit: Matteo Piazza</label></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 0px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Philadelphia-Navy-Yard.jpg&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Philadelphia-Navy-Yard.jpg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"https://www.asla.org/2014awards/326.html\"><h2>Reuse</h2></a><p>The Navy abandoned Philadelphia's Navy Yard in the mid-1990s but left a rich legacy of infrastructure and buildings that became the headquarters for Urban Outfitters. D.I.R.T. Studio salvaged left-over materials, reworking them into something boldly new. </p><label class=\"bylineText\">2014 ASLA Professional General Design Honor Award. Urban Outfitters Headquarters at the Philadelphia Navy Yard, Philadelphia, Pennslyvania. D.I.R.T. Studio / D.I.R.T. Studio</label></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 0px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/residential-2015.jpg&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/residential-2015.jpg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"https://www.asla.org/2014awards/380.html\"><h2>Residential Design</h2></a><p>In Sagaponack, New York, the Atlantic Ocean is slowly encroaching due to climate change. To escape rising tides, a couple moved their house 400 feet inland. There, LaGuardia Landscape Architects recreated the historic coastal landscape of dunes and meadows.</p><label class=\"bylineText\">ASLA 2013 Professional Residential Design Award of Excellence. Sagaponack Residence. Sagaponack, New York. LaGuardia Design Landscape Architects / image credit: Eva Cocco</label></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 0px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Tech-Town.jpg&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Tech-Town.jpg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"https://www.asla.org/2014awards/055.html\"><h2>Urban Revitalization</h2></a><p>Through an ambitious new plan, a multi-disciplinary team at Sasaki Associates is helping to revitalize TechTown, a knowledge district in midtown Detroit. The goal is to create a hub for innovation and collaboration through improvements to the public realm.</p><label class=\"bylineText\">ASLA 2014 Professional Analysis and Planning Award of Excellence. Midtown Detroit Techtown District. Detroit, Michigan. Sasaki Associates, Inc. / image credit: Sasaki Associates</label></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 0px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Woodland-Rain-Garden.jpg&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Woodland-Rain-Garden.jpg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"https://www.asla.org/2014awards/602.html\"><h2>Rain Gardens</h2></a><p>Caddo Parish, Louisiana, gets 5 to 6 feet of rain every year. Instead of flushing that water out into a ravine, Jeffrey Carbo Landscape Architects devised a beautiful system of rainwater harvesting and drainage that makes visible the movement of water through the landscape.</p><label class=\"bylineText\">ASLA 2014 Professional Residential Award of Excellence. Woodland Rain Gardens. Caddo Parish, Louisiana. Jeffrey Carbo Landscape Architects / image credit: Rebecca O'Neal</label></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 0px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Orongo-Master-Plan.jpg&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Orongo-Master-Plan.jpg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"https://www.asla.org/2010awards/205.html\"><h2>Ecological Restoration</h2></a><p>At Young Nick's Head, a peninsula on the east coast of New Zealand, Nelson Byrd Woltz Landscape Architects are transforming a 3,000-acre sheep farm into a wildlife sanctuary. To improve biodiversity, both saltwater and freshwater wetlands are being restored.</p><label class=\"bylineText\">ASLA 2010 Professional Analysis and Planning Honor Award. Orongo Station Conservation Master Plan. New Zealand. Nelson Byrd Woltz Landscape Architects / image credit: Nelson Byrd Woltz Landscape Architects</label></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 0px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Rooftop-Haven.jpg&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Rooftop-Haven.jpg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"https://www.asla.org/2010awards/377.html\"><h2>Green Roofs</h2></a><p>This green roof in Chicago not only cools the air and absorbs stormwater, but also produces 1,000 pounds of organic food annually. Hoerr Schaudt Landscape Architects designed this haven for the Gary Comer Youth Center to also be a learning environment.</p><label class=\"bylineText\">ASLA 2010 Professional General Design Honor Award. Rooftop Haven for Urban Agriculture, Chicago, Illinois. Hoerr Schaudt Landscape Architects / image credit: Scott Shigley</label></div></li><li aria-hidden=\"true\" style=\"height: 0px;\"><div class=\"uk-cover-background uk-position-cover\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Lafitte-Corridor.jpg&quot;);\"></div><img src=\"/uploadedImages/CMS/HomePage_New/Lafitte-Corridor.jpg\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; opacity: 0;\"><div class=\"uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-background\"><a href=\"https://www.asla.org/2013awards/328.html\"><h2>Transportation</h2></a><p>In New Orleans, the 3-mile-long Lafitte Greenway, covering some 50 acres of barren land, will become a sustainable transportation corridor. Landscape architecture firm Design Workshop worked with the city government to fully envision a linear green park.</p><label class=\"bylineText\">ASLA 2013 Professional Analysis and Planning Award of Excellence. Lafitte Greenway + Revitalization Corridor. New Orleans, Louisiana. Design Workshop, Inc. / image credit: Design Workshop, Inc.</label></div></li></ul>\n\n            <a href=\"\" class=\"uk-slidenav showArrow\" data-uk-slideshow-item=\"previous\">\n
